<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g175932g0610031750615.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AstroNova Reports Fiscal First-Quarter 2022 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Product Identification bookings hit all time high </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First-Quarter Fiscal 2022 Summary </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Bookings of $32.8&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Backlog at quarter end of $24.8&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue of $29.1&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Operating income of $0.7&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net income of $0.6&nbsp;million, or $0.08 per diluted share </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Adjusted EBITDA of $2.5&nbsp;million, or 8.6% of revenue </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>WEST WARWICK, R.I. &#151; June</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;10, 2021 &#151; </B>AstroNova, Inc. (NASDAQ: ALOT), a global leader in data visualization technologies,
today announced financial results for the fiscal 2022 first quarter ended May&nbsp;1, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Revenue was generally in line with our expectations in
the first quarter compared with last year, as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> growth in the Product Identification segment partly offset Aerospace industry-related weakness in the Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment due to the
effects of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic and continued weakness in 737 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">MAX-related</FONT> shipments,&#148; said Gregory A. Woods, President and Chief Executive Officer of AstroNova.
&#147;Bookings came in ahead of last year&#146;s level, with Product Identification posting a new record and our Aerospace bookings increasing 45% sequentially to mark the first positive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">book-to-bill</FONT></FONT> ratio since fiscal 2020. We continued to carefully manage expenses in the quarter, which allowed us to maintain profitability and improve overall margins despite lower revenue. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Q1 marked another strong quarter for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T3-OPX,</FONT> our wide-format durable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">direct-to-package</FONT></FONT> printing system, which continues to exceed expectations,&#148; Woods said. &#147;Our Product Identification segment had solid results, particularly in Europe, reflecting our recent sales
reorganization in the EMEA region.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q1 FY 2022 Operating Segment Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Product Identification segment revenue was $23.1&nbsp;million, compared with $22.4&nbsp;million in the prior-year period. Segment operating income was
$2.7&nbsp;million, or 11.8% of revenue, compared with $3.1&nbsp;million, or 14.1% of revenue, in the prior year, primarily due to higher operating costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment revenue was $6.0&nbsp;million, compared with $8.5&nbsp;million in the same period of fiscal 2021. The decrease reflected
lower aerospace printer sales associated with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> and the 737 MAX impact. The Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment recorded an operating profit of $0.4&nbsp;million, or 5.9% of revenue, compared with
segment operating loss of $0.2&nbsp;million, or negative 1.8% of revenue, in the comparable period of fiscal 2021, reflecting lower manufacturing costs and operating expense. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Hardware revenue was $7.6&nbsp;million in the fiscal 2022 first quarter, compared with $8.9&nbsp;million in
the prior-year period, as lower Aerospace shipments in the Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement segment more than offset growth in Product Identification. Supplies revenue was $18.2&nbsp;million versus $19.1&nbsp;million in the same period of fiscal 2021. In
fiscal 2021, demand for Aerospace supplies was strong in early Q1, while Product Identification supplies picked up later in the quarter as customers added to their stocks of the Company&#146;s inks, labels and other materials because of concerns
about the pandemic. Service/other revenue was $3.2&nbsp;million, compared with $2.9&nbsp;million a year earlier. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q1 FY 2022 Results Summary </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue totaled $29.1&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2022, compared with $30.9&nbsp;million in the year-earlier period, with a decline in
Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement revenue partly offset by higher revenue in the Product Identification segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit was $10.9&nbsp;million, or 37.4%
of revenue in the first quarter of fiscal 2022, compared with $10.9&nbsp;million, or 35.1% of revenue, in the same period of fiscal 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating
expenses totaled $10.2&nbsp;million in the first quarters of fiscal 2022 and 2021, and operating income was $0.7&nbsp;million in both periods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income
was $0.6&nbsp;million, or $0.08 per diluted share, in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 compared with net income of $0.4&nbsp;million, or $0.06 per diluted share, in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted EBITDA, which the Company defines as earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization and share-based compensation, was $2.5&nbsp;million
for the first quarter of fiscal 2022, or 8.6% of revenue, compared with $2.6&nbsp;million, or 8.3% of revenue, in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. Adjusted EBITDA is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure explained in
greater detail below under &#147;Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measure.&#148; Please refer to the financial reconciliation table included in this news release for a reconciliation of net income to Adjusted EBITDA
for the three months ended May&nbsp;1, 2021 and May&nbsp;2, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bookings in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 were $32.8&nbsp;million, compared with
$31.2&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Backlog as of May&nbsp;1, 2022 was $24.8&nbsp;million versus $25.9&nbsp;million at the end of the
fiscal 2021 first quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Earnings Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova will discuss its fiscal first-quarter 2022 financial results in an investor conference call at 9:00 a.m. ET today. To participate on the conference
call, please dial (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">367-2403</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (334) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">777-6978</FONT> (International) approximately 10 minutes prior to the start time and enter confirmation code
8107119. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You can hear a replay of the conference call from 12:00 p.m. ET Thursday, June&nbsp;10, 2021 until 12:00 p.m. ET on Thursday, June&nbsp;17, 2021
by dialing (888) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">203-1112</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (719) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">457-0820</FONT> (International). The passcode is 8107119. A real-time and an archived audio webcast of the call will be
available through the &#147;Investors&#148; section of the AstroNova website, https://investors.astronovainc.com. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measure </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to financial measures prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), this news release contains the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure Adjusted EBITDA, which AstroNova defines as earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization and share-based compensation. AstroNova believes that the inclusion of this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure helps investors gain a meaningful understanding of changes in the Company&#146;s core operating results, and also can help investors who wish to make comparisons between AstroNova and
other companies on both a GAAP and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis. AstroNova&#146;s management uses Adjusted EBITDA, in addition to GAAP financial measures, as the basis for measuring its core operating performance and
comparing such performance to that of prior periods and to the performance of its competitors. Adjusted EBITDA also is used by the Company&#146;s management to assist with their financial and operating decision-making. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About AstroNova </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova, Inc. (NASDAQ: ALOT), a global
leader in data visualization technologies since 1969, is focused on designing, manufacturing, distributing and servicing a broad range of products that acquire, store, analyze and present data in multiple formats. The Company&#146;s Product
Identification segment offers a complete <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">line-up</FONT> of label and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">direct-to-package</FONT></FONT> printing hardware and supplies, allowing
customers to mark, track and enhance their products&#146; appearance. Supported by AstroNova&#146;s customer application experts and technology leadership in printing, material science and high-speed data processing, customers benefit from an
optimized, &#147;total solution&#148; approach. The Test and Measurement segment includes the AstroNova Aerospace business unit. This segment designs and manufactures flight deck printers, networking hardware and related accessories serving the
world&#146;s aerospace and defense industries with proven advanced airborne technology solutions for the cockpit, the cabin and so much more. AstroNova is a member of the Russell Microcap<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>
Index and the LD Micro Index (INDEXNYSEGIS: LDMICRO). Additional information is available by visiting&nbsp;<U>www.astronovainc.com</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Information included in this
news release may contain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. Forward-looking statements are not statements of historical fact but rather reflect our current expectations concerning
future events and results. These statements may include the use of the words &#147;believes,&#148; &#147;expects,&#148; &#147;intends,&#148; &#147;plans,&#148; &#147;anticipates,&#148; &#147;likely,&#148; &#147;continues,&#148; &#147;may,&#148;

or achievements to be materially different from those expressed or implied by such forward-looking statements. These risks, uncertainties and factors include, but are not limited to, those factors set forth in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on

any forward-looking statements, whether as a result of new information, future events or otherwise. The reader is cautioned not to unduly rely on such forward-looking statements when evaluating the information presented in this news release. </P>
